<div id="nextra-skip-nav"></div><main data-pagefind-body="true"><h1 class="x:tracking-tight x:text-slate-900 x:dark:text-slate-100 x:font-bold x:mt-2 x:text-4xl"><code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">_meta.js</code> File</h1>
<p class="x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7">In Nextra, the site and individual page structure can be configured via the
co-located <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">_meta</code> files. Those configurations affect the overall layout of your
Nextra theme, especially the navigation bar and the sidebar:</p>
<figure class="mt-[1.25em]"><span aria-owns="rmiz-modal-721e19de0c1b" data-rmiz=""><span data-rmiz-content="found" style="visibility: visible;"><img alt="Example of Nextra Theme Docs" data-pagefind-index-attrs="title,alt" loading="lazy" width="1671" height="1034" decoding="async" data-nimg="1" class="nextra-border rounded-xl border drop-shadow-sm" srcset="/_next/image?url=%2F_next%2Fstatic%2Fmedia%2Frouting%401x.3f040172.png&amp;w=1920&amp;q=75 1x, /_next/image?url=%2F_next%2Fstatic%2Fmedia%2Frouting%401x.3f040172.png&amp;w=3840&amp;q=75 2x" src="/_next/image?url=%2F_next%2Fstatic%2Fmedia%2Frouting%401x.3f040172.png&amp;w=3840&amp;q=75" style="color: transparent;"></span><span data-rmiz-ghost="" style="height: 516px; left: 410px; width: 832px; top: 296px;"><button aria-label="Expand image: Example of Nextra Theme Docs" data-rmiz-btn-zoom="" type="button"><svg aria-hidden="true" data-rmiz-btn-zoom-icon="true" fill="currentColor" focusable="false" viewBox="0 0 16 16" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M 9 1 L 9 2 L 12.292969 2 L 2 12.292969 L 2 9 L 1 9 L 1 14 L 6 14 L 6 13 L 2.707031 13 L 13 2.707031 L 13 6 L 14 6 L 14 1 Z"></path></svg></button></span></span><figcaption class="mt-2 text-center text-sm">Example: <a class="x:focus-visible:nextra-focus x:text-primary-600 x:underline x:hover:no-underline x:decoration-from-font x:[text-underline-position:from-font]" href="/docs/docs-theme">Nextra Docs Theme</a> has sidebar and navbar generated automatically from Markdown files.</figcaption></figure>


<h2 id="organizing-files" class="x:tracking-tight x:text-slate-900 x:dark:text-slate-100 x:font-semibold x:target:animate-[fade-in_1.5s] x:mt-10 x:border-b x:pb-1 x:text-3xl nextra-border">Organizing files<a href="#organizing-files" class="x:focus-visible:nextra-focus subheading-anchor" aria-label="Permalink for this section"></a></h2>
<p class="x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7">Nextra allows you to organize files in the following ways:</p>
<ul class="x:[:is(ol,ul)_&amp;]:my-[.75em] x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:list-disc x:ms-[1.5em]">
<li class="x:my-[.5em]">
<p class="x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7"><strong>In Next.js’
<a href="https://nextjs.org/docs/app/getting-started/project-structure#top-level-folders" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" class="x:focus-visible:nextra-focus x:text-primary-600 x:underline x:hover:no-underline x:decoration-from-font x:[text-underline-position:from-font]"><code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">app</code> directory</a>:</strong><br>Nextra
gathers all <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">page</code> files, including
<a class="x:focus-visible:nextra-focus x:text-primary-600 x:underline x:hover:no-underline x:decoration-from-font x:[text-underline-position:from-font]" href="/docs/file-conventions/page-file"><code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">page.md</code> and <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">page.mdx</code> files</a> as well as
<code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">_meta</code> files.</p>
</li>
<li class="x:my-[.5em]">
<p class="x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7"><strong>In Nextra’s
<a class="x:focus-visible:nextra-focus x:text-primary-600 x:underline x:hover:no-underline x:decoration-from-font x:[text-underline-position:from-font]" href="/docs/file-conventions/content-directory"><code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">content</code> directory</a>:</strong><br>Nextra
collects all <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">.md</code> and <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">.mdx</code> files, along with <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">_meta</code> files.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p class="x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7">Below the same file-based routing structure is represented for <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">content</code> and
<code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">app</code>-only directories:</p>

<p class="x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7">You can combine both organizational ways for your project:</p>
<ul class="contains-task-list">
<li class="task-list-item"><input disabled="" type="checkbox" checked=""> the <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">content</code> directory with <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">.mdx</code> files</li>
<li class="task-list-item"><input disabled="" type="checkbox" checked=""> the <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">app</code> directory with <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">page</code> files</li>
</ul>
</div></div>
<h3 id="pagemap-structure" class="x:tracking-tight x:text-slate-900 x:dark:text-slate-100 x:font-semibold x:target:animate-[fade-in_1.5s] x:mt-8 x:text-2xl"><code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">pageMap</code> structure<a href="#pagemap-structure" class="x:focus-visible:nextra-focus subheading-anchor" aria-label="Permalink for this section"></a></h3>
<p class="x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7">Afterward, Nextra generates a <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">pageMap</code> array containing information about your
entire site’s routes and directories structure. Features such as the navigation
bar and sidebar can be generated based on the <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">pageMap</code> information.</p>
<p class="x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7">The generated <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">pageMap</code> will be:</p>
<div data-pagefind-ignore="all" class="nextra-code x:relative x:not-first:mt-[1.25em]"><div class="x:px-4 x:text-xs x:text-gray-700 x:dark:text-gray-200 x:bg-gray-100 x:dark:bg-neutral-900 x:flex x:items-center x:h-12 x:gap-2 x:rounded-t-md x:border x:border-gray-300 x:dark:border-neutral-700 x:contrast-more:border-gray-900 x:contrast-more:dark:border-gray-50 x:border-b-0"><svg viewBox="0 0 30 10" fill="currentColor" stroke="none" height="1em" class="x:max-w-6 x:shrink-0"><path d="M30 0V10H28L26 4V10H24V0H26L28 6V0H30Z"></path><path d="M20.3335 10H17.6665C17.2247 9.9995 16.8011 9.82376 16.4887 9.51134C16.1762 9.19892 16.0005 8.77533 16 8.3335V1.6665C16.0005 1.22467 16.1762 0.801082 16.4887 0.488662C16.8011 0.176241 17.2247 0.000502876 17.6665 0H20.3335C20.7753 0.000502876 21.1989 0.176241 21.5113 0.488662C21.8238 0.801082 21.9995 1.22467 22 1.6665V8.3335C21.9995 8.77533 21.8238 9.19892 21.5113 9.51134C21.1989 9.82376 20.7753 9.9995 20.3335 10ZM18 8H20V2H18V8Z"></path><path d="M12.3335 10H8V8H12V6H10C9.46973 5.99947 8.96133 5.78859 8.58637 5.41363C8.21141 5.03867 8.00053 4.53027 8 4V1.6665C8.0005 1.22467 8.17624 0.801082 8.48866 0.488662C8.80108 0.176241 9.22467 0.000502876 9.6665 0H14V2H10V4H12C12.5303 4.00053 13.0387 4.21141 13.4136 4.58637C13.7886 4.96133 13.9995 5.46973 14 6V8.3335C13.9995 8.77533 13.8238 9.19892 13.5113 9.51134C13.1989 9.82376 12.7753 9.9995 12.3335 10Z"></path><path d="M4.3335 10H1.6665C1.22467 9.9995 0.801082 9.82376 0.488662 9.51134C0.176242 9.19892 0.000502876 8.77533 0 8.3335V6H2V8H4V0H6V8.3335C5.9995 8.77533 5.82376 9.19892 5.51134 9.51134C5.19892 9.82376 4.77533 9.9995 4.3335 10Z"></path></svg><span class="x:truncate">pageMap</span></div><pre class="x:group x:focus-visible:nextra-focus x:overflow-x-auto x:subpixel-antialiased x:text-[.9em] x:bg-white x:dark:bg-black x:py-4 x:ring-1 x:ring-inset x:ring-gray-300 x:dark:ring-neutral-700 x:contrast-more:ring-gray-900 x:contrast-more:dark:ring-gray-50 x:contrast-more:contrast-150 x:rounded-b-md not-prose" tabindex="0"><div class="x:group-hover:opacity-100 x:group-focus:opacity-100 x:opacity-0 x:transition x:focus-within:opacity-100 x:flex x:gap-1 x:absolute x:right-4 x:top-14"><button class="x:transition x:cursor-pointer x:border x:border-gray-300 x:dark:border-neutral-700 x:contrast-more:border-gray-900 x:contrast-more:dark:border-gray-50 x:rounded-md x:p-1.5 x:md:hidden" title="Toggle word wrap" type="button" data-headlessui-state=""><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" height="1em"><path d="M4 19h6v-2H4v2zM20 5H4v2h16V5zm-3 6H4v2h13.25c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2s-.9 2-2 2H15v-2l-3 3l3 3v-2h2c2.21 0 4-1.79 4-4s-1.79-4-4-4z"></path></svg></button></div><code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr"><span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">[</span></span>
<span><span style="--shiki-light: #6A737D; --shiki-dark: #6A737D;">  // content/_meta.js</span></span>
<span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">  { </span><span style="--shiki-light: #005CC5; --shiki-dark: #79B8FF;">"data"</span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">: {} },</span></span>
<span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">  {</span></span>
<span><span style="--shiki-light: #6A737D; --shiki-dark: #6A737D;">    // content/index.mdx</span></span>
<span><span style="--shiki-light: #005CC5; --shiki-dark: #79B8FF;">    "name"</span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light: #032F62; --shiki-dark: #9ECBFF;">"index"</span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">,</span></span>
<span><span style="--shiki-light: #005CC5; --shiki-dark: #79B8FF;">    "route"</span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light: #032F62; --shiki-dark: #9ECBFF;">"/"</span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">,</span></span>
<span><span style="--shiki-light: #005CC5; --shiki-dark: #79B8FF;">    "title"</span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light: #032F62; --shiki-dark: #9ECBFF;">"Index"</span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">,</span></span>
<span><span style="--shiki-light: #005CC5; --shiki-dark: #79B8FF;">    "frontMatter"</span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">: {}</span></span>
<span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">  },</span></span>
<span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">  {</span></span>
<span><span style="--shiki-light: #6A737D; --shiki-dark: #6A737D;">    // content/contact.md</span></span>

<span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">  },</span></span>
<span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">  {</span></span>
<span><span style="--shiki-light: #6A737D; --shiki-dark: #6A737D;">    // content/about</span></span>
<span><span style="--shiki-light: #005CC5; --shiki-dark: #79B8FF;">    "name"</span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light: #032F62; --shiki-dark: #9ECBFF;">"about"</span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">,</span></span>
<span><span style="--shiki-light: #005CC5; --shiki-dark: #79B8FF;">    "route"</span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light: #032F62; --shiki-dark: #9ECBFF;">"/about"</span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">,</span></span>
<span><span style="--shiki-light: #005CC5; --shiki-dark: #79B8FF;">    "title"</span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light: #032F62; --shiki-dark: #9ECBFF;">"About"</span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">,</span></span>

<span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">      {</span></span>

<span><span style="--shiki-light: #005CC5; --shiki-dark: #79B8FF;">        "route"</span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light: #032F62; --shiki-dark: #9ECBFF;">"/about"</span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">,</span></span>
<span><span style="--shiki-light: #005CC5; --shiki-dark: #79B8FF;">        "title"</span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light: #032F62; --shiki-dark: #9ECBFF;">"Index"</span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">,</span></span>

<span><span style="--shiki-light: #005CC5; --shiki-dark: #79B8FF;">        "title"</span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light: #032F62; --shiki-dark: #9ECBFF;">"Legal"</span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">,</span></span>
<span><span style="--shiki-light: #005CC5; --shiki-dark: #79B8FF;">        "frontMatter"</span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">: {}</span></span>
<span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">      }</span></span>

<span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">]</span></span></code></pre></div>
<p class="x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7">And the global <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">pageMap</code> will be imported to each page by Nextra. Then,
configured theme will render the actual UI with that <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">pageMap</code>.</p>
<h2 id="api" class="x:tracking-tight x:text-slate-900 x:dark:text-slate-100 x:font-semibold x:target:animate-[fade-in_1.5s] x:mt-10 x:border-b x:pb-1 x:text-3xl nextra-border">API<a href="#api" class="x:focus-visible:nextra-focus subheading-anchor" aria-label="Permalink for this section"></a></h2>
<p class="x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7">The title and order of a page shown in the sidebar/navbar can be configured in
the <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">_meta</code> file as key-value pairs.</p>

<h3 id="title-type" class="x:tracking-tight x:text-slate-900 x:dark:text-slate-100 x:font-semibold x:target:animate-[fade-in_1.5s] x:mt-8 x:text-2xl"><code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">title</code> type<a href="#title-type" class="x:focus-visible:nextra-focus subheading-anchor" aria-label="Permalink for this section"></a></h3>
<p class="x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7">When specifying a <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">title</code> in <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">_meta</code> file, you can define it as either a simple
string or a JSX element.</p>
<div data-pagefind-ignore="all" class="nextra-code x:relative x:not-first:mt-[1.25em]"><pre class="x:group x:focus-visible:nextra-focus x:overflow-x-auto x:subpixel-antialiased x:text-[.9em] x:bg-white x:dark:bg-black x:py-4 x:ring-1 x:ring-inset x:ring-gray-300 x:dark:ring-neutral-700 x:contrast-more:ring-gray-900 x:contrast-more:dark:ring-gray-50 x:contrast-more:contrast-150 x:rounded-md not-prose" tabindex="0"><div class="x:group-hover:opacity-100 x:group-focus:opacity-100 x:opacity-0 x:transition x:focus-within:opacity-100 x:flex x:gap-1 x:absolute x:right-4 x:top-2"><button class="x:transition x:cursor-pointer x:border x:border-gray-300 x:dark:border-neutral-700 x:contrast-more:border-gray-900 x:contrast-more:dark:border-gray-50 x:rounded-md x:p-1.5 x:md:hidden" title="Toggle word wrap" type="button" data-headlessui-state=""><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" height="1em"><path d="M4 19h6v-2H4v2zM20 5H4v2h16V5zm-3 6H4v2h13.25c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2s-.9 2-2 2H15v-2l-3 3l3 3v-2h2c2.21 0 4-1.79 4-4s-1.79-4-4-4z"></path></svg></button></div><code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr"><span><span style="--shiki-light: #D73A49; --shiki-dark: #F97583;">type</span><span style="--shiki-light: #6F42C1; --shiki-dark: #B392F0;"> TitleSchema</span><span style="--shiki-light: #D73A49; --shiki-dark: #F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light: #005CC5; --shiki-dark: #79B8FF;"> string</span><span style="--shiki-light: #D73A49; --shiki-dark: #F97583;"> |</span><span style="--shiki-light: #6F42C1; --shiki-dark: #B392F0;"> ReactElement</span></span></code></pre></div>
<p class="x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7">For the below file structure:</p>

<h4 id="type-page-option" class="x:tracking-tight x:text-slate-900 x:dark:text-slate-100 x:font-semibold x:target:animate-[fade-in_1.5s] x:mt-8 x:text-xl"><code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">type: 'page'</code> option<a href="#type-page-option" class="x:focus-visible:nextra-focus subheading-anchor" aria-label="Permalink for this section"></a></h4>
<p class="x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7">By defining a top-level page or folder as <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr"><span data-line=""><span style="--shiki-light: #6F42C1; --shiki-dark: #B392F0;">type</span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light: #032F62; --shiki-dark: #9ECBFF;">'page'</span></span></code>, it will be shown
as a special page on the navigation bar, instead of the sidebar. With this
feature, you can have multiple “sub docs”, and special pages or links such as
“Contact Us” that are always visible.</p>
<p class="x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7">For example, you can have 2 docs folders <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">frameworks</code> and <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">fruits</code> in your
project. In your top-level <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">_meta</code> file, you can set everything as a page,
instead of a normal sidebar item:</p>

<h4 id="display-hidden-option" class="x:tracking-tight x:text-slate-900 x:dark:text-slate-100 x:font-semibold x:target:animate-[fade-in_1.5s] x:mt-8 x:text-xl"><code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">display: 'hidden'</code> option<a href="#display-hidden-option" class="x:focus-visible:nextra-focus subheading-anchor" aria-label="Permalink for this section"></a></h4>
<p class="x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7">By default, all MDX routes in the filesystem will be shown on the sidebar. But
you can hide a specific pages or folders by using the <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr"><span data-line=""><span style="--shiki-light: #6F42C1; --shiki-dark: #B392F0;">display</span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light: #032F62; --shiki-dark: #9ECBFF;">'hidden'</span></span></code>
configuration:</p>
<div data-pagefind-ignore="all" class="nextra-code x:relative x:not-first:mt-[1.25em]"><div class="x:px-4 x:text-xs x:text-gray-700 x:dark:text-gray-200 x:bg-gray-100 x:dark:bg-neutral-900 x:flex 24" fill="currentColor" height="1em" class="x:max-w-6 x:shrink-0"><path d="M21.8182 0H2.18182C0.976364 0 0 0.976364 0 2.18182V21.8182C0 23.0236 0.976364 24 2.18182 24H21.8182C23.0236 24 24 23.0236 24 x:lg:top-1/2 x:lg:right-full x:lg:-translate-y-1/2"></a><code class="nextra-code x:max-md:break-all x:after:content-[&quot;?&quot;]" dir="ltr">typesetting</code></td><td class="x:p-3 x:max-lg:block x:max-lg:before:content-[&quot;Type:_&quot;]"><code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">"default,article"</code><div class="x:mt-2"><p class="x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7">Configures the text typesetting style.</p></div></td><td class="x:max-lg:block x:py-3 x:max-lg:pt-0 x:max-lg:px-3 x:max-lg:before:content-[&quot;Default:_&quot;]"><code class="nextra-code x:whitespace-pre-wrap x:inline-block" dir="ltr">'default'</code></td></tr></tbody></table>
<h5 id="layouts" class="x:tracking-tight x:text-slate-900 x:dark:text-slate-100 x:font-semibold x:target:animate-[fade-in_1.5s] x:mt-8 x:text-lg">Layouts<a href="#layouts" class="x:focus-visible:nextra-focus subheading-anchor" aria-label="Permalink for this section"></a></h5>
<p class="x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7">By default, each page has <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr"><span data-line=""><span style="--shiki-light: #6F42C1; --shiki-dark: #B392F0;">layout</span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light: #032F62; --shiki-dark: #9ECBFF;">'default'</span></span></code> in their theme config, which
is the default behavior. You might want to render some page with the full
container width and height, but keep all the other styles. You can use the
<code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr"><span data-line=""><span style="--shiki-light: #032F62; --shiki-dark: #9ECBFF;">'full'</span></span></code> layout to do that:</p>
<div data-pagefind-ignore="all" class="nextra-code x:relative x:not-first:mt-[1.25em]"><div class="x:px-4 x:text-xs x:text-gray-700 x:dark:text-gray-200 x:bg-gray-100 x:dark:bg-neutral-900 x:flex <h5 id="typesetting-section" class="x:tracking-tight x:text-slate-900 x:dark:text-slate-100 x:font-semibold x:target:animate-[fade-in_1.5s] x:mt-8 x:text-lg">Typesetting<a href="#typesetting-section" class="x:focus-visible:nextra-focus subheading-anchor" aria-label="Permalink for this section"></a></h5>
<p class="x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7">The <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">typesetting</code> option controls typesetting details like font features,
heading styles and components like <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">&lt;li&gt;</code> and <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">&lt;code&gt;</code>. There are
<code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr"><span data-line=""><span style="--shiki-light: #032F62; --shiki-dark: #9ECBFF;">'default'</span></span></code> and <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr"><span data-line=""><span style="--shiki-light: #032F62; --shiki-dark: #9ECBFF;">'article'</span></span></code> typesettings available in the docs theme.</p>
<p class="x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7">The default one is suitable for most cases like documentation, but you can use
the <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr"><span data-line=""><span style="--shiki-light: #032F62; --shiki-dark: #9ECBFF;">'article'</span></span></code> typesetting to make it look like an elegant article page:</p>

type="button" data-headlessui-state=""><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" height="1em"><path d="M4 19h6v-2H4v2zM20 5H4v2h16V5zm-3 6H4v2h13.25c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2s-.9 2-2 2H15v-2l-3 3l3 <span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">  about: {</span></span>

<span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">    }</span></span>
<span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">  }</span></span>

<h3 id="folders" class="x:tracking-tight x:text-slate-900 x:dark:text-slate-100 x:font-semibold x:target:animate-[fade-in_1.5s] x:mt-8 x:text-2xl">Folders<a href="#folders" class="x:focus-visible:nextra-focus subheading-anchor" aria-label="Permalink for this section"></a></h3>
<p class="x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7">Folders can be configured in the same way as pages.</p>
<p class="x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7">For example, the following top-level <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">_meta</code> file contains the meta information
for the top-level pages and folders.<br> The nested <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">_meta</code> file contains the
meta information for pages in the same folder:</p>
<div class="flex gap-2 *:last:w-full *:last:min-w-0 max-lg:flex-wrap"><ul class="nextra-filetree x:mt-[1.25em] x:select-none x:text-sm x:text-gray-800 x:dark:text-gray-300 not-prose x:rounded-lg 0-2-2H9a2 2 0 0 0-2 2v5a2 2 0 0 1-2 2Z"></path></svg>app</button><ul class="x:flex x:flex-col x:gap-2 x:ps-4"><li class="x:flex x:flex-col x:gap-1"><button class="x:transition x:cursor-pointer x:flex x:items-center x:gap-1 x:break-all x:text-start" type="button" data-headlessui-state=""><svg fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" height="14" class="x:shrink-0"><path stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" d="M3 7v10a2 2 0 0 0 2 2h14a2 2 0 0 0 2-2V9a2 2 0 0 0-2-2h-6l-2-2H5a2 2 0 0 0-2 2Z"></path></svg>[[...mdxPath]]</button></li><li class="x:flex x:items-center <div class="nextra-callout x:overflow-x-auto x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:flex x:rounded-lg x:border x:py-[.5em] x:pe-[1em] x:contrast-more:border-current! x:bg-blue-100 x:dark:bg-blue-900/30 x:text-blue-700 x:dark:text-blue-400 x:border-blue-700 x:dark:border-blue-600"><div class="x:select-none x:text-[1.25em] x:ps-[.6em] x:pe-[.4em]" data-pagefind-ignore="all" style="font-family: &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;"><svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="currentColor" height=".8em" class="x:mt-[.3em]"><path d="M0 8a8 8 0 1 1 16 0A8 8 0 0 1 0 8Zm8-6.5a6.5 6.5 0 1 0 0 13 6.5 6.5 0 0 0 0-13ZM6.5 7.75A.75.75 0 0 1 7.25 7h1a.75.75 0 0 1 .75.75v2.75h.25a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-2a.75.75 0 0 1 0-1.5h.25v-2h-.25a.75.75 0 0 1-.75-.75ZM8 6a1 1 0 1 1 0-2 1 1 0 0 1 0 2Z"></path></svg></div><div class="x:w-full x:min-w-0"><b>Note</b>
<p class="x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7">You can move directories around without having to change the <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">_meta</code> file
since information for pages are grouped together in directories.</p>
</div></div>
<h4 id="with-index-page" class="x:tracking-tight x:text-slate-900 x:dark:text-slate-100 x:font-semibold x:target:animate-[fade-in_1.5s] x:mt-8 x:text-xl">With <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">/index</code> page<a href="#with-index-page" class="x:focus-visible:nextra-focus subheading-anchor" aria-label="Permalink for this section"></a></h4>
<p class="x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7">To create a folder with an index page, add <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr"><span data-line=""><span style="--shiki-light: #6F42C1; --shiki-dark: #B392F0;">asIndexPage</span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light: #005CC5; --shiki-dark: #79B8FF;">true</span></span></code> to its front
matter.</p>
<p class="x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7">For example, to create a <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">/fruits</code> route, setting <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr"><span data-line=""><span style="--shiki-light: #6F42C1; --shiki-dark: #B392F0;">asIndexPage</span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light: #005CC5; --shiki-dark: #79B8FF;">true</span></span></code> tells
Nextra that <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">/fruits</code> is a folder with an index page. Clicking the folder in the
sidebar will expand it and display the MDX page.</p>
<div class="flex gap-2 *:last:w-full *:last:min-w-0 max-lg:flex-wrap"><ul class="nextra-filetree x:mt-[1.25em] x:select-none x:text-sm x:text-gray-800 x:dark:text-gray-300 not-prose x:rounded-lg <h3 id="menus" class="x:tracking-tight x:text-slate-900 x:dark:text-slate-100 x:font-semibold x:target:animate-[fade-in_1.5s] x:mt-8 x:text-2xl">Menus<a href="#menus" class="x:focus-visible:nextra-focus subheading-anchor" aria-label="Permalink for this section"></a></h3>
<p class="x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7">You can also add menus to the navbar using <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr"><span data-line=""><span style="--shiki-light: #6F42C1; --shiki-dark: #B392F0;">type</span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light: #032F62; --shiki-dark: #9ECBFF;">'menu'</span></span></code> and the <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">items</code>
option:</p>

<span><span style="--shiki-light: #D73A49; --shiki-dark: #F97583;">type</span><span style="--shiki-light: #6F42C1; --shiki-dark: #B392F0;"> MenuSchema</span><span style="--shiki-light: #D73A49; --shiki-dark: #F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;"> {</span></span>

<h3 id="fallbacks" class="x:tracking-tight x:text-slate-900 x:dark:text-slate-100 x:font-semibold x:target:animate-[fade-in_1.5s] x:mt-8 x:text-2xl">Fallbacks<a href="#fallbacks" class="x:focus-visible:nextra-focus subheading-anchor" aria-label="Permalink for this section"></a></h3>
<p class="x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7">In the <a href="#type-page-option" class="x:focus-visible:nextra-focus x:text-primary-600 x:underline x:hover:no-underline x:decoration-from-font x:[text-underline-position:from-font]"><code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr"><span data-line=""><span style="--shiki-light: #6F42C1; --shiki-dark: #B392F0;">type</span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light: #032F62; --shiki-dark: #9ECBFF;">'page'</span></span></code> option</a> above, we have to define
the <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr"><span data-line=""><span style="--shiki-light: #6F42C1; --shiki-dark: #B392F0;">type</span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light: #032F62; --shiki-dark: #9ECBFF;">'page'</span></span></code> option for every page. To make it easier, you can use
the <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">'*'</code> key to define the fallback configuration for all items in this folder:</p>
<div data-pagefind-ignore="all" class="nextra-code x:relative x:not-first:mt-[1.25em]"><div class="x:px-4 x:text-xs x:text-gray-700 x:dark:text-gray-200 x:bg-gray-100 x:dark:bg-neutral-900 x:flex 21.8182V2.18182C24 0.976364 23.0236 0 21.8182 0ZM12 17.8691C12 19.8076 10.8109 20.8942 8.83636 20.8942C6.88582 20.8942 5.64327 19.7542 5.64327 17.9105H7.75636C7.76182 18.5945 8.16982 19.0265 8.80036 <p class="x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7">They are equivalent where all items have <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr"><span data-line=""><span style="--shiki-light: #6F42C1; --shiki-dark: #B392F0;">type</span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light: #032F62; --shiki-dark: #9ECBFF;">'page'</span></span></code> set.</p>
<h3 id="_metaglobal-file" class="x:tracking-tight x:text-slate-900 x:dark:text-slate-100 x:font-semibold x:target:animate-[fade-in_1.5s] x:mt-8 x:text-2xl"><code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">_meta.global</code> file<a href="#_metaglobal-file" class="x:focus-visible:nextra-focus subheading-anchor" aria-label="Permalink for this section"></a></h3>
<p class="x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7">You can also define all your pages in a single <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">_meta</code> file, suffixed with
<code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">.global</code>. The API remains the same as for folder-specific <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">_meta</code> files, with 1
exception: <strong>folder items must include an <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">items</code> field</strong>.</p>
<p class="x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7">For the following structure, you might use the following <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">_meta</code> files:</p>

</div></div>
<h2 id="good-to-know" class="x:tracking-tight x:text-slate-900 x:dark:text-slate-100 x:font-semibold x:target:animate-[fade-in_1.5s] x:mt-10 x:border-b x:pb-1 x:text-3xl nextra-border">Good to know<a href="#good-to-know" class="x:focus-visible:nextra-focus subheading-anchor" aria-label="Permalink for this section"></a></h2>
<h3 id="sorting-pages" class="x:tracking-tight x:text-slate-900 x:dark:text-slate-100 x:font-semibold x:target:animate-[fade-in_1.5s] x:mt-8 x:text-2xl">Sorting pages<a href="#sorting-pages" class="x:focus-visible:nextra-focus subheading-anchor" aria-label="Permalink for this section"></a></h3>
<p class="x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7">You can use ESLint’s built-in <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">sort-keys</code> rule, append
<code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">/* eslint sort-keys: error */</code> comment at the top of your <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">_meta</code> file, and you
will receive ESLint’s errors about incorrect order.</p>
<h3 id="type-of-_meta-keys" class="x:tracking-tight x:text-slate-900 x:dark:text-slate-100 x:font-semibold x:target:animate-[fade-in_1.5s] x:mt-8 x:text-2xl">Type of <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">_meta</code> keys<a href="#type-of-_meta-keys" class="x:focus-visible:nextra-focus subheading-anchor" aria-label="Permalink for this section"></a></h3>
<p class="x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7">The type of your <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">_meta</code> keys should always <strong>be a string</strong> and <strong>not a number</strong>
because
<a href="https://dev.to/frehner/the-order-of-js-object-keys-458d" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" class="x:focus-visible:nextra-focus x:text-primary-600 x:underline x:hover:no-underline x:decoration-from-font x:[text-underline-position:from-font]">numbers are always ordered first&nbsp;<svg fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="1.7" viewBox="0 0 24 24" height="1em" class="x:inline x:align-baseline x:shrink-0"><path d="M7 17L17 7"></path><path d="M7 7h10v10"></path></svg></a>
in JavaScript objects.</p>
<p class="x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7">For example, consider the following:</p>
<div data-pagefind-ignore="all" class="nextra-code x:relative x:not-first:mt-[1.25em]"><div class="x:px-4 x:text-xs x:text-gray-700 x:dark:text-gray-200 x:bg-gray-100 x:dark:bg-neutral-900 x:flex x:items-center x:h-12 x:gap-2 x:rounded-t-md x:border x:border-gray-300 x:dark:border-neutral-700 x:contrast-more:border-gray-900 x:contrast-more:dark:border-gray-50 x:border-b-0"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" height="1em" class="x:max-w-6 x:shrink-0"><path d="M21.8182 0H2.18182C0.976364 0 0 0.976364 0 2.18182V21.8182C0 23.0236 0.976364 24 2.18182 24H21.8182C23.0236 24 24 23.0236 24 21.8182V2.18182C24 0.976364 23.0236 0 21.8182 0ZM12 17.8691C12 19.8076 10.8109 20.8942 8.83636 20.8942C6.88582 20.8942 5.64327 19.7542 5.64327 17.9105H7.75636C7.76182 18.5945 8.16982 19.0265 8.80036 19.0265C9.44836 19.0265 9.79636 18.6185 9.79636 17.8505V11.9978H12V17.8691ZM17.9793 20.8942C15.7876 20.8942 14.4087 19.8622 14.3716 18.1931H16.4727C16.5262 18.8236 17.1556 19.2251 18.0687 19.2251C18.8913 19.2251 19.4564 18.8291 19.4564 18.2585C19.4564 17.7785 19.0778 17.52 18.0873 17.3225L16.9473 17.0945C15.3622 16.7945 14.5462 15.9305 14.5462 14.568C14.5462 12.8749 15.9033 11.7644 17.9913 11.7644C20.0204 11.7644 21.4244 12.8629 21.4604 14.4655H19.4258C19.3778 13.8535 18.7953 13.4269 18.0196 13.4269C17.2462 13.4269 16.7367 13.7935 16.7367 14.3695C16.7367 14.844 17.1207 15.12 18.0327 15.3L19.1476 15.516C20.8593 15.8465 21.6273 16.62 21.6273 17.9945C21.6284 19.8022 20.2484 20.8942 17.9793 20.8942Z"></path></svg><span class="x:truncate">_meta.js</span></div><pre class="x:group x:focus-visible:nextra-focus x:overflow-x-auto x:subpixel-antialiased x:text-[.9em] x:bg-white x:dark:bg-black x:py-4 x:ring-1 x:ring-inset x:ring-gray-300 x:dark:ring-neutral-700 x:contrast-more:ring-gray-900 x:contrast-more:dark:ring-gray-50 x:contrast-more:contrast-150 x:rounded-b-md not-prose" tabindex="0"><div class="x:group-hover:opacity-100 x:group-focus:opacity-100 <span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">  foo: </span><span style="--shiki-light: #032F62; --shiki-dark: #9ECBFF;">''</span><span style="--shiki-light: #24292E; --shiki-dark: #E1E4E8;">,</span></span>

<p class="x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7">will be converted to:</p>

<div data-pagefind-ignore="all" class="nextra-code x:relative x:not-first:mt-[1.25em]"><div class="x:px-4 x:text-xs x:text-gray-700 x:dark:text-gray-200 x:bg-gray-100 x:dark:bg-neutral-900 x:flex <p class="x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7">The <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">.js</code>, <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">.jsx</code>, or <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">.tsx</code> file extensions can be used for <code class="nextra-code" dir="ltr">_meta</code> file.</p>
